mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张海涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年出生，河南省南阳市镇平县籍人，原<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代国企下岗工人，新疆区域电信产品销售者、自由职业者，民主人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市中亚南路派出所警方以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”抄家、刑事拘留、逮捕；之后被以“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，羁押于新疆乌鲁木齐市看守所。据悉，其家中银行卡全部被警方冻结，妻子即将生育，生活面临极大困境。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被变更罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续超期关押，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被乌鲁木齐中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家罪”、“为境外刺探、非法提供情报罪”重判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日经新疆乌鲁木齐高级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔族自治区沙雅监狱九监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张慧岩：原</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省通化市柳河县白酒厂技术员，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，流离失所十年的法轮功学员张慧岩被抓捕。当年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，家属接到公主岭监狱电话才得知，张慧岩被柳河县判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被送进吉林省公主岭市监狱，目前已两个多月，家人不允许见面。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张健：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。张健于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被长春市二道公安分局东盛路派出所抓捕，在苇子沟拘留所被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日后送至长春市第三看守所，转为刑事拘留，后被朝阳区检察院起诉。听说张健现在被非法关押在宋家新建的一个羁押场所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张健家属得到有关部门通知，张健被视频开庭，非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#211226224726-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#211226224726-2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张建华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江加格达奇法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被加格达奇曙光派出所抓捕。知情人说，因为张建华给人讲真相，被跟踪，被警察抄家并抓捕。警察从她家里抢走法轮功相关书籍等私人财产。因警察抢劫现金，张建华的儿子制止。几天后，她儿子竟被以“袭警”为名抓捕。家人费尽周折，儿子才被放回。张建华一直被羁押在加格达奇看守所，后被加格达奇区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日早被送往黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445762.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445762.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张建中：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，天津市人，职业不详，“反腐义勇军”工作室负责人，实名举报人，民主维权公民，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年以来，因其一直实名举报天津开发区（滨海新区）泰达俱乐部董事长董文胜<span lang="EN-US">(</span>在押）等人，将国有资产变相流失及勾结公安人员违法乱纪等行为，故而屡遭天津公权部门（含滨海新区及河北区法院等）灭绝人性式的打压摧残和逼迫；曾因长期在反腐和推进民主法治等维权运动中被多次软禁及饱受人权被践踏之苦，而导致被开除公职，并一直被中共当局标暗号为“贩毒”人员，剥夺其居住权、低保权和婚姻存续权；期间，曾多次遭警察殴打，打至骨折并致残，迄今重病缠身，生活极度贫困；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其因长期揭露中共恶行，预料可能随时会被再次抓捕，故而在网上公开发表“绝不自杀”声明；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因关注人权律师“王全璋案”而去天津市第二中级法院围观和参加旁听，而被天津市河北区墙子派出所警方拦截带走，后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘、逮捕，并被关押在天津市河北区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，被天津市河北区法院以其在“<span lang="EN-US">facebook</span>发布或转发涉及国内重大事件、严重损害国家形像等不实帖文，混淆视听，起哄闹事，造成恶劣的社会影响，严重扰乱了公共秩序”为由，以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出狱后，其依然遭受着公权力的打压和迫害；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因其应江苏省昆山市维权人士王和英之邀，欲于次日乘高铁前往昆山参加王定于<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日的“和盈茶庄”的开业，而被辖区的警察拦截软禁<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又因六四将至，紧接着是中共建党一百周年，为求维稳，遂河北区警方在其居所附近距离几米处，紧急安装了一组监控摄像头；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，获悉其于六四前夕又被天津市河北区警方带走，自此失联，后经网友确认，知其已被河北区警方正式刑拘，涉嫌罪名暂不明晰。目前被羁押于天津市河北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_58.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_58.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张荆州：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，原湖北省荆州市金隆集团公司员工，法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，张荆州已被处罚<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次：<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚上，荆州市公安局指挥，沙市开发区公安局和燎原派出所十几个警察在出租屋，抓捕了张荆州与邵廉，并抄家，抢走打印纸<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十多箱，打印机约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>台，电脑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台，还有裁纸刀等物品。张荆州、邵廉被关押在荆州西门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，张荆州被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邵廉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">连市<span lang="EN-US">123</span>中学教师、法轮功学员。张军与妻子苗玉环都在大连市<span lang="EN-US">123</span>中学工作。张军是体育教师，妻子苗玉环是高级音乐教师。张军夫妇一九九九年以前开始修炼法轮功。从一九九九年“七·二零”中共、发动对法轮功的疯狂迫害以后，他们夫妇曾经三次被抓捕，十几次被区政法委、教育局、登沙河派出所骚扰，被金普新区教委迫害扣发工资。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，张军被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，他被普兰店法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、罚款八千元。张军已上诉到大连市中级法院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/21/445216.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/21/445216.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张筠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈阳市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，女。张筠老太太，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>只眼睛已失明，另<span lang="EN-US">1</span>只视力也很差，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被几个警察关押、做核酸检验和体检，并于次日被于洪区法院庭审，当天送沈阳市第一看守所。据悉，张筠老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，但家属并没有收到判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">张俊玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。吉林珲春市残疾妇女，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被强行做核酸检测后关押到延吉看守所，是坐轮椅进去的。后得知，张俊玲在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初坐轮椅被关押到吉林省女子监狱。监狱目前不让家属接见，家人们心急如焚，非常担心她的身体情况。后获悉张俊玲又被判刑一年半。中共人员给家属的说法是：在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年那年判的刑不算了，原因是没在关押中，在家中不算。所以从这次，也就是<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日送进看守所之日开始算，整个刑期<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张君琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，宁夏固原市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共恶党开始疯狂迫害法轮功，张君琴因坚持修炼，遭受中共邪党抓捕、关押、劳教，而后被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，流离失所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多，回家不久的张君琴女士，被固原市原州区国保大队警察抓捕，被关押迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，张君琴被固原市原州区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张亢<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">云南玉溪市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">.</span>毕业于西南师范大学，二零一五年八月份，参加玉溪华宁教育系统考试合格，考取华宁县的教师岗位，二零一五年九月，到华宁县偏远山区彝族苗族自治县通红甸乡华宁第九中学担任中学语文教师。张亢因为坚持信仰法轮功，不写所谓的“三书”，华宁县第九中学校领导，在华宁县教育局不法人员的授意下，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，以一年满为借口，解聘张亢老师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日其母亲任惠萍发法轮功真相资料，被绑架到红塔分局。当天深夜十一点多，玉溪市红塔分局国保大队到任会萍家，抄家，警察以打印机是张亢的为借口，在凌晨一点多，抓捕了张亢及抢走家里的私人物品。任惠萍、张亢母女俩被非法关押在红塔区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被玉溪市江川县法院视频开庭，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日任惠萍、张亢均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张昆山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 50</span>多岁。辽宁朝阳市凌源市法轮功学员，原为凌源钢铁公司职工。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，朝阳市公安局，政法委，<span lang="EN-US">610</span>秘密开会策划迫害，预谋在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，要抓一批法轮功学员，向中共百年大庆“献礼”；并成立专项行动小组，电话监控，跟踪监视。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，朝阳市出动大批警力在同一时间对朝阳市法轮功学员及家属实施抓捕、抄家抢劫。据不完全统计，至少有<span lang="EN-US">27</span>名法轮功学员及家属被抓捕。凌源市公安局及派出所动用了大约<span lang="EN-US">50</span>名警察，抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名凌源市法轮功学员。张昆山是其中之一，被关押在凌源市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被凌源市法院远程视频开庭。后得知：张昆山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张兰英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">天津公开退党第一人、维权人士。原是中国建设银行的一名中层管理人员，因自家房屋被南开区政府强拆强占而维权，在南开区当局的迫害下使其家破人亡。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，张兰英以书面形式向中共中央组织部及当地相关部门提出退出中共组织的请求，但未获得相关部门的回复；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，张兰英以视频公开的形式控诉当地政府对她的迫害并提出退党声明，她是天津公开退党第一人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年张被当地法院以莫须有罪名判囚三年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，张兰英服刑期间她的父亲含冤去世，至今仍冰冻在殡仪馆无法下葬；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，张兰英刑满释放后得知中国建设银行早已将其除名。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，张兰英因在国家信访局信访遭到天津市南开区学府街派出所警员带回后，当地警方指控张兰英在其微博发布自己的冤情，该微博转发量达<span lang="EN-US">500+</span>、以及网络媒体对她的冤情报道及其进京在国家信访局登记控诉。天津市公安局南开分局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”将张刑事拘留，已被当地检察院批捕，目前张兰英羁押于天津市南开区看守所正被警方补充侦查。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张莉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张莉有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张立娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林伊通县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，吉林省伊通县法轮功学员张立娟和她儿子曹博宇分别在自家附近和家中被吉林省辽源市国保警察马队长等人秘密抓捕，关押在辽源市看守所。警察又抄家，劫走法轮功书籍、法相、资料、电脑、打印机、订书器等大量私人物品。曹博宇被关押近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月左右被放回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，辽源市西安区法院视频开庭，张立娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张立君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">黑龙江省双鸭山法轮功学员、双鸭山市石油公司职工、法轮功学员张立君女，<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁，据因给公检法警察邮寄法轮功宣传信，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被双鸭山市公安局、尖山分局等单位抓捕，羁押在双鸭山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日遭双鸭山尖山检察院批捕。卷宗目前打回尖山分局补充侦查。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张莉敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邓玉林、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。张莉敏刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张立云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林榆树市青山乡法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上十点多钟，张立云在日升村发放真相资料时，被村长刘景伟劫持到派出所。后被抓捕到拘留所、看守所，拒收；又被关押在公安局隔离。隔离之后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被关押到榆树市看守所。之后被构陷到德惠市检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张立云被德惠市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，关押在到吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E6%A6%86%E6%A0%91%E5%B8%82%E9%9D%92%E5%B1%B1%E4%B9%A1%E5%BC%A0%E7%AB%8B%E4%BA%91%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-434444.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E6%A6%86%E6%A0%91%E5%B8%82%E9%9D%92%E5%B1%B1%E4%B9%A1%E5%BC%A0%E7%AB%8B%E4%BA%91%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-434444.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张立新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江大庆市被迫流离失所的法轮功学员。丈夫白玉福是原大庆市石油管理局测井公司武保科科长；妻子张立新，原大庆石油管理局物业二公司乘风热力分公司职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，白玉福和张立新开始修炼法轮功，按真、善、忍标准做好人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，白玉福、张立新夫妇多次被中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，白玉福、张立新夫妇在辽宁省阜新市彰武县被警方抓捕，后刑事拘留、批捕、起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被彰武县法院视频开庭。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉，白玉福被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，张立新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。张立新刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，张立新在阜新市新地看守所被迫害致脑出血，经抢救，保住了生命，肌肉已开始萎缩，保外就医被拒。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张美玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，山东烟台法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，烟台市莱山区公安局有预谋的绑架了十几名法轮功学员，关押在烟台市福山看守所。其中张美玲、孙鼎美遭受八个月的关押、构陷后，被判刑，张美玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；孙鼎美<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初宣判后，张美玲、孙鼎美上诉烟台市中级法院。烟台市中级法院二审维持原判。张美玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/27/2022-5-27.html#22526225225-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/27/2022-5-27.html#22526225225-2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张梦颖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，河北省石家庄市高新区宋营镇南辛庄村人，农民，遭强拆受害者，实名举报人，全国百万“出嫁女”群体维权代表，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。早在<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾因婚后户口未从婚前所在村庄地址迁出，而被当地毫无法律效力的《村规民约》中的男女不平观念和陋习所制约，使其应享有同村同等的村民待遇权利（即集体经济组织成员权利）被剥夺；其被迫举报维权，求公道，但历经<span lang="EN-US"> 16</span>年之久依然未能给予妥善解决，反倒因其不断控诉和呼吁而屡遭地方当局报复与逼迫；后在其不断维权抗争中结识到众多与其命运相同的“出嫁女”，故而逐步成长为全国百万“出嫁女”群体的维权代表；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因宋营镇南辛庄村委会以“村民自治”为借口，剥夺了其及同村多名“出嫁女” 依法应享有的同等集体经济收益分配权，随其数人联名发《致石家庄市人民政府市长艾文礼的公开信》，以期政府部门尽快解决他们应该享有的村民同等待遇权利的三点要求，即“<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、关于到今后失地农民的养老保险问题；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、关系到我们失去土利地今后的一份生活保障；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、集体经济收益就是我们失去土地后的一份生活来源的保障”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因其多次遭地方乡镇官员阻止维权和强打强压，使其及家人苦不堪言，其本人亦被迫流浪在外，其随在北京钓鱼台国宾馆割腕自杀，以示抗议，不料当其被救并被石家庄驻京办遣回原籍后，其家耕地被强占，树木被损坏；其为此投诉、呼吁讨说法，但镇政府对其遭遇却回复说：“国家法律是一回事，底下是另一回事，男女就不能平等”；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾数年来多次向纪检委、检察院等各级部门反应、举报地方官员贪污腐败及收受贿赂等事宜，但都被石家庄市高新区管理者当局压案不查，随其再次向国家纪检委等部门举报当地官员为集体利益和小金库而贪赃枉法，并表明根据法律“村民自治根本不存在”，申请中央亲自来调查；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被突然撬门闯进的石家庄市警方莫名抓走，其家遭查抄；次日，即被以不具名罪名刑拘，至今未予释放；据悉，其被抓捕，疑与在中共“两会”期间和“三八妇女节”前夕，其向与会代表、委员们吁请中共政府兑现<span lang="EN-US">40</span>多年来“生男生女一个样”的承诺，及同时要求全国人大常委会取消河北省王东峰、石家庄市委书记张超超的全国人大代表资格有关。目前疑被羁押于石家庄市看守所。。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_98.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_98.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张明毅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省南京市玄武区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。，江苏省金陵石化建安公司职工，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮大法，身心受益。后曾三次在洗脑班、两次在精神病院被关押迫害，一次被非法劳教二年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在单位办公室被警察绑架带走，随后被抄家，抄走了打印机及真相资料等私人物品，后一直被非法关押。直到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在苏州监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张慕杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，北京法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，祖籍北京延庆，孤身一人居住在北京大兴区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日清晨，张慕杰被闯入家中的清源路派出所吴姓警察抓捕。警察抢走法轮功台历九十本左右，内夹真相期刊等。张慕杰被关押在大兴看守所。清源派出所吴姓警察对张慕杰进一步构陷和批捕。张慕杰已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被大兴区法院秘密非法判刑四年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张乃君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功遭当局长期打压迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，当其在鞍山市铁西区兴盛街道附近粘贴法轮功资料时，遭到铁西区兴盛街道办事处工作人员白英涛的恶意举报，遂被鞍山市铁西区兴盛派出所警方很快以涉嫌宣传邪教罪抓捕，次日被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日已被鞍山市铁西区检察院以同罪名正式批捕。被羁押于鞍山市第一看守所。后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日又遭抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被庭审。刑期未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张盼成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1995</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，甘肃省庆阳市合水县人，网名为“子慕予兮”，中国西北农村长大留守儿童，前北京大学保安，正义公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早年出生于甘肃农村，是典型的留守儿童；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾以公民身份表达自己的意愿；在辞去北京大学保安工作之后，曾放胆自拍视频，发政治主张，称已为民主“做好了牺牲的准备”；被捕前，曾在视频中表示，不同意中国政府将<span lang="EN-US">600</span>亿美元未经法定程序送<span lang="EN-US">(</span>外国）人，要求言论自由，声援被失踪的董瑶琼、华涌、佳士工人和原北大学生岳昕等人，以及进学习班的百万新疆同胞；曾在视频中引用宋代名将文天祥的诗句“人生自古谁无死，留取丹心照汗青”，并说自己对国家有深沉的爱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；审讯中，拒绝写保证书，并拒绝给律师签委托书；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其案在北京西城区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被北京市西城区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其在网上发布一段在甘肃山村老家里录制的视频，谴责中共暴行，表达心声称“凛凛寒冬终将过去，春天马上要来临”，随后被当地警方带走，后知又被当地合县检察院转正式批捕，被关押在甘肃省庆阳市合水县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，知其已被甘肃省合水县法院一审秘判，但其家人未获判决书；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日本网获悉，其似被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。目前在甘肃省武都监狱（甘肃省武都区吉石坝武都监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">746000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/3-3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/3-3.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">35</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岁左右，本科学历，不论是在家乡还是在单位都是受人称赞的热心青年。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">咸阳市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员</span>张鹏、王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏因为向淳化县民众发放真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月先后在各自的住所被淳化县公安局警察抓捕抄家。张鹏、王钰超（<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁左右）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底在咸阳市住处被警察绑架，电脑、打印机等设备被抢走。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位法轮功学员被关押在咸阳淳化县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均已被判刑，其中张鹏判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏约为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年不等，刑期不详。张鹏刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副总经理、温泉度假村经理。孙大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：张平被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张强：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，辽宁省营口市人，<span lang="EN-US">89</span>六四亲历者，无身份证黑户人，前广州市某美国贸易公司重要职员，网络活跃人士<span lang="EN-US">,</span>社会热点事件关注者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年，张强曾就读于华南理工大学化工机械系高分子机械专业；<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月毕业之际，却因参与<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学运，要出门上街时被院系领导拦下，随后以“学习成绩不好”为由被学校开除，并其在校户籍亦被该校联合派出所偷偷注销，自此，使之成为一个彻底的无身份证黑户人（又称“隐形人”），以致长期不能到正规单位工作、不能乘坐火车、飞机，无法办理结婚登记，以及所有凡与身份证件相关的事宜都无法成行或着办成；之后，其曾为此将广州市公安局告上法庭，该案曾两次开庭审理，但都以其无身份证而被拒进入法庭参加庭审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，因张强曾在朋友圈和微信群里发信息质疑了当地警局某领导的死因，遂被广东省广州市海珠区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，又被广州市海珠区检察院亦同罪名予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案被海珠区警方移送至海珠区检察院审查起诉，期间，延长审查起诉期限一次；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案在广州市海珠区法院开庭审理；据悉，检察院建议对其量刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前张强被羁押于广州市海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_10.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_10.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，家住上海市徐汇区，原是上海市胜德塑料有限公司的技术骨干，曾任总工程师、质监科科长等职务。一九九四年九月开始修炼法轮。张勤因为坚持信仰曾经两次被判刑，刑期分别为<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，还被劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张勤又遭逮捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，张勤被上海奉贤区法院庭审、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，借口是“累犯重判”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: minor-fareast;">1942</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张勤被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张任飞<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，张任飞等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括张任飞在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。张任飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省辛集市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span
