italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京市密云区新城子镇法轮功学员。家住北京市密云区新城子镇曹家路村。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，陈志华、张玉华夫妇被抓捕、抄家，关押在密云区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈志华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，张玉华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/8/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432292p.html#2110722010-9"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/8/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432292p.html#2110722010-9</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张玉莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省南阳市法轮功学员，年过七旬。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，张玉莲曾两次被判刑，累计陷冤狱七年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河南省南阳市公安局统一行动，在南阳地区开始大面积绑架法轮功学员。两陷冤狱的七旬法轮功学员张玉莲老太再被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，张玉莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，勒索罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张玉明：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张玉明被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张玉萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西太原市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年约六十岁，家庭妇女，一九九八年十月开始修炼法轮大法，一九九九年七月中共迫害法轮功后，她多次遭骚扰、抄家、抓捕，曾被劳教及判刑。因兑换真相币给便利店，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚被太原市文庙派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被太原市迎泽区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三万。张玉萍关押在古交第四看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/20/%E5%B1%B1%E8%A5%BF%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%BC%A0%E7%8E%89%E8%90%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440291.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/20/%E5%B1%B1%E8%A5%BF%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%BC%A0%E7%8E%89%E8%90%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440291.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张岳兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省南通市如皋市人，南通市如皋市如城街道西郊居九组<span lang="EN-US">70</span>号公民，维权公民，公益举报人，中国在押维权人士。早年，曾因其房屋遭政府强拆而被迫上访维权，后在上访过程中逐渐成长为维权公民，并开始致力于关注公益维权事业；自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，曾因举报江苏省如皋市公交违规收费事宜，而如皋市政府和相关部门却一直并未履行法定职责查处和纠正这一违法行为，故而随后其又举报了多个公共场所长期违反消防法占用消防疏散信道经营等违法事项；尽管其举报意图旨在为了社会公益，但地方当局及职能部门却为了自身的集团利益，无视其举报的相关问题，公然失职渎职，维护违反消防法、占用消防车信道和疏散信道等现象，甚至层层谎报，拒不整改、消除障碍及依法查处问题所在；由于如皋市当局对其举报多年的违法事实不予理会也不立案查处，因而为了掩盖政府部门的不作为和乱作为（即几次出现谎报现象），遂长期高薪雇佣多个保安非法限制其人身自由，并将其住所用钢材焊死，非法安装监视器，对其全天候的拍照与跟踪；其虽多次报警但无果；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其因担心电瓶车长久不充电耗损电瓶（因正被长期软禁中），故而到车库欲给电瓶车充电，但竟被监控者跟着，一脚踹开车库门，将其殴打致伤；其即刻电话报警，不料如皋市警方反将其带走，被莫名处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转为刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被如皋市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案被地方检察院起诉并移交到江苏省南通市如皋市法院；至今，未审待判；据悉，其律师认为其不构成寻衅滋事罪，已向检察院提交不起诉意见书。目前被羁押于江苏省如皋市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_92.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_92.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代出生，陕西省籍人，上海市浦东新区常驻居民，网络异见人士，公民记者、民主公民。硕士学位，毕业后即在上海谋职工作；因不满中共政府的政治现状，长期在网络平台发布批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，其做派活跃、内容尖锐而颇具针对性，故而曾多次被上海市警方约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因其在微信等网络平台大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是每天自己撰文发声，利用行为艺术等为声援香港举牌，随于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海警方传唤，自此失联，后知其被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，其父因受警方威胁，故对外拒透其具体信息；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终获释放；据悉，羁押期间，其曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”。此前被羁押于上海市浦东新区看守所。张展自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日左右去到武汉报导当地疫情，一直在微信、推特、<span lang="EN-US">YouTube </span>等社交媒体平台上直播武汉的现场情况，并尽其所能地帮助受疫情影响的人维权。张展在武汉实地写了大量关于武汉疫情的真实报道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在武汉遭“强迫失踪”，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被上海市浦东分局刑事拘留，被控罪名是寻衅滋事，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。被起诉，其在狱中绝食抗议，身体状况极差。至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展的妈妈说，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日视频中看到最大的不同是张展身体明显好了一些，也比较牵挂父母家人。张展愿意在监狱里面做一些手工。她开始自主进食，不再被灌食；以前因为长期绝食肠胃比较疼痛，现在肠胃有所恢复；她可以独立行走，不需要他人搀扶。视频通话<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟后结束，张展也请父母保重身体。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现羁押在浦东新区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，张展女士案一审开庭，并当庭宣判，张展女士因言获罪被上海浦东新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_13.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_13.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张珍华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川达州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。四川省万源市茶品公司的退休职工。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，张珍华正在友人毛坤家做客休息，又被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点半，被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">张志兰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，河北省唐山市丰南区法轮功学员。家住唐山市丰润区小张各庄镇南青坨村。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，张志兰开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日早上五点，唐山市公安局伙同小张各庄派出所警察从邻居家跳墙翻入张志兰家，抓捕了还在熟睡的她。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，在南滦法院庭审。张志兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张志江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赤峰市元宝山区五家镇小石头分金桥村居民，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚在大水清道上被喀喇沁旗楼子店派出所警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午，赤峰元宝山区五家镇村警领着锦山公安局警察闯到张志江家非法抄家，在家里没人的情况下，搜走了大法书。并将张志江非法关押在喀喇沁旗锦山看守所。之后，喀喇沁旗公安局编造材料，将构陷张志江的案卷上报到喀喇沁旗检察院，检察院以张志江炼法轮功、悬挂真相条幅等理由，非法起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，内蒙古赤峰市喀喇沁旗法院开庭非法庭审法轮功学员张志江。张志江为自己做了无罪辩护。法院随后将张志江非法判刑，具体刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">章兴连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日早上，四川泸州市法轮功学员敖启珍、唐祖群、彭昭群、章兴连四人从各自家中被抓捕，随后被抄家，关押看守所，被江阳区法院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，泸州市江阳区法院以惯用的诬陷罪名对四人判刑：唐祖群、敖启珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元；彭昭群、章兴连被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金八千元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，泸州市中级法院对唐祖群、敖启珍、章兴连、彭昭群四名法轮功学员，下达维持泸州市江阳区法院一审原判的裁定。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-13"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-13</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵爱真</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东菏泽法轮功学员，女，生于<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年，菏泽市牡丹区糖果食品厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日傍晚，王翠英在路边发送真相册子时，被跟踪监控的牡丹区公安局警察抓捕。当日晚上，国保大队警察闯入独居的赵爱真家中，将她抓捕，并抄家，将家中的两台电脑、三台打印机、大法书、真相资料、光盘、打印纸等大量个人物品尽数抄走。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，王翠英、赵爱真两人被牡丹区公安分局刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，遭批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，鄄城县法院下的判决，王翠英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款两万元；赵爱真被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万五千元。赵爱真刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵晨宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">昆明市女教师、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁，原是昆明市第三十中学一级教师，中文系研究生，是一位学生爱戴的好老师。赵晨宇曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。赵晨宇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初回西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市探望年迈的母亲，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日刚返回到昆明家中，就被跟踪而来的西双版纳景洪市国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在西双版纳再次被庭审，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。被关押在西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk54972182"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。赵根法刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵国爱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵海军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，黑龙江省哈尔滨市人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因信仰法轮功，并与其妻等人为中共镇压、迫害法轮功到北京和平请愿，被当局抓捕，先被关押于哈尔滨双城市看守所，后又被送到双城区单城敬老院进行强制洗脑教育，期间因屡受虐待酷刑愤而绝食抗议，当局才不得不于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月将其释放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因前往北京为法轮功进行和平请愿，而被北京警方抓捕，并被关押于北京市团河劳教所，直至一年多后方予以释放。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因其屡次控告迫害法轮功的元凶江泽民，遂被当地警方从家中抓走，并被以涉邪教罪刑拘，其家遭查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被双城区检察院转正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨双城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后虽经哈尔滨市中级法院二审，但依然维持原判。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱服刑。据悉，因在狱中遭遇虐待，致其长期不能排尿而被强制打针。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵海通：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，青海省海西州人，新疆民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。因长期致力于为新疆地区弱势群体、维吾尔族群体及政治犯、良心犯等维权呼吁，近年来又南下广东，积极与南方各地维权公民、人权捍卫者等一起参与街头民主运动，举行各种声援举牌和集会活动，故而在所处之地备受民众欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因前往湖北武汉会见人权活动家秦永敏，惨遭武汉警方的野蛮殴打，差点丧命；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因努力表达维权公民正当合法的诉求，而不惧风险在广州火车站多次举牌，宣传民主理念，“抗议流氓政府打压民主人士”等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因参与声援安徽民主人士张林之女张安妮失学事件，而遭警方强行拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因在新疆吐鲁番市帮助维吾尔族公民进行维权，而被新疆警方刑拘，并被关押于新疆乌鲁木齐市六道湾看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被新疆警方宣布以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，终被新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院以同罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市乌苏市乌苏监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵恒德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏法轮功学员。生于<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，原系宁夏隆德县卫生局干部，近几年居住在宁夏银川市。赵恒德<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上，发放法轮功资料，被警察抓捕。在当天晚上十点左右，警察到他家抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，赵恒德被银川市公安局兴庆区分局刑拘，关押在银川市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，赵恒德被逮捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，他被银川市公安局兴庆区分局警察构陷到银川市西夏区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，赵恒德在银川市西夏区法院被开庭。北京维权律师为他做了有理有据的无罪辩护，要求无罪释放。后被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，至今他被关押在银川市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/15/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E8%B5%B5%E6%81%92%E5%BE%B7%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441298.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/15/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E8%B5%B5%E6%81%92%E5%BE%B7%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441298.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵怀国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">基督徒，湖南省张家界市慈利县常驻居民，慈利县伯特利基督教会建立人，伯利恒教会主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。因笃信基督，而于，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起从从东北到湖南省慈利县传福音，同年创办伯特利家庭教会，信徒多以年长者为主；因其所属教会曾多次被官方要求加入“三自教会”，均因价值理念不合而被其及教会众信徒拒绝，遂成为当局排挤、维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾遭大批公安警方及宗教局人员闯入教会打砸；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，慈利县宗教局曾出动县民族宗教事务局、公安局、城管等部门近<span lang="EN-US">50</span>人，强行撬开伯特利教会大门，毁坏教会用品，撕毁墙上宗教信仰标志，并抄走《圣经》、诗歌本福音单张、钢琴等各类教会用品；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被张家界市慈利县警方突然以涉嫌’煽动颠覆国家政权罪’刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被慈利县检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因使用翻墙软件浏览境外媒体有关武汉疫情的报导，又转发嘲讽政府的打油诗等文字，属于严重危害国家安全行为；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其“煽动颠覆国家政权罪” 案在张家界市中级法院开庭受审，公诉方建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，法官称将择日宣判。目前疑被羁押于慈利县看守所（湖南省张家界市慈利县零阳镇，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">427200</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，抚顺市新宾县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，赵杰和另一法轮功学员走在路上，被抚顺市新宾县公安局国保大队和派出所警察抓捕，在抚顺市第一看守所被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金两万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">赵景兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺市望花区古城子法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁，<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日在南沟集市宣传法轮功，遭国保及古城子派出所抓捕。家属去古城子派出所等相关部门要人，没有人接待。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月家属得知赵景兰被望花法院秘密判决<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年刑期，关押在抚顺市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk54973417"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵俊香：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54973417;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省庆云县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，山东省庆云县公安局国保大队纠集几十个警察，抓捕了正在学习法轮大法著作的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多名法轮功学员。根据长期电话监听和监控，警察又抓捕<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，共计<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人，其中大多数是<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的老人，大部份法轮功学员被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，在庆云县法院，夏津县法院人员对六名仍被关押的庆云法轮功学员，赵俊香、王素娟、杜全村、段桂霞、于炳兰、张连云庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东夏津县法院开出判决书：赵俊香判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，杜全村判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王素娟判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于炳兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，张连云判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。赵俊香刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵丽华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：赵丽华被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵丽英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川内江法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，原在四川内江市铁路机务段小学教书，已退休，现居住内江铁路机械学校家属宿舍。在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，赵丽英在内江市区贴法轮功传单，被内江市中区公安分局派人跟踪，抓捕，并抄家，被关押到内江市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，赵丽英被构陷到了内江检察院。之后，家人、朋友一直没有得到任何信息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底，赵丽英已经被非押一年多，家人去给她送衣物时，才被看守所人员告知，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，赵丽英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款二千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员，哈尔滨市轴承厂退休职工，现年已经七十岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，赵林在南岗区先锋路附近粘贴了一张“法轮大法好”不干胶，被南岗公安分局国保警察抓捕、抄家，抢走其家中法轮大法书籍。后获悉被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵林（河北）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北张家口市桥东区法轮功学员。赵林<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午被张家口市公安局桥东分局<span lang="EN-US">51</span>路派出所警察抓捕，并抄走手机维修小店工作用的计算机，同时抄走法轮功资料。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，桥西区法院定对赵林开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月赵林被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵美华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邯郸法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，赵美华被复兴区刑警队和铁路大院派出所警察抓捕，被关押在邯郸第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，邯郸市磁县法院对赵美华视频开庭。后得知，赵美华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵美君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省淮南市法轮功学员。女，安徽省淮南市潘集区泥河镇大郢村人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被蚌埠市怀远县国保大队绑架强行带走。警察抢走家里所有法轮功有关的东西，包括<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台打印机和一些大法真相资料和半成品和纸张等等，共拉走皮卡车一车。后经蚌埠市淮上法院，赵美君被判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冻结资金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万多元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/12/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432451.html#211011205037-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/12/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432451.html#211011205037-1</span></b></a></span><b mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵仁霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生。山东省青岛法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午五点左右，赵仁霞从住处下楼，被青岛开发区公安分局国保大队警察绑架，而后把赵转移到户口管辖地灵珠山派出所。<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午五点左右，灵珠山派出所警察将赵押到青岛市普东看守所羁押。后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，赵仁霞被青岛市黄岛区法院判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵任远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西桂林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日半夜，谢建新与妻子赵任远被桂林市七星分局的派出所警察声称“测体温”闯入家中，搜查抄走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>轮功书籍、资料、法轮功币等物品，并抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵树霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市滨海新区大港法轮功学，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功以来，赵树霞因为坚持修炼法轮功，曾被多次迫害，先后两次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次判刑，累计遭冤狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年多。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被劳教时她绝食抗议<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，身体极度虚弱，期间被强行灌食，冬天包夹犯人把窗户打开折磨她。最后她被迫害致生命垂危，最后警察无奈放人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，赵树霞去天津市区办事，被天津市南开区国保抓捕、关押，然后警察又到大港赵树霞的母亲家抄家。有知情人透露，抓捕构陷她的原因只是因为她给警察写了一封劝善信。后两次被开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬获悉她已被劫持到天津女子监狱。据家人说她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/7/445902.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/7/445902.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵淑芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年出生，内蒙古自治区呼伦贝尔市莫力达瓦达斡尔族自治旗（莫旗）人，满族，呼伦贝尔市莫旗中心商店下岗职工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月起，因笃信和宣传法轮功，曾屡遭内蒙古自治区自扎兰屯市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室、国保大队警方及公检法司法部门等的监控、打压和逼迫；曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被劳教，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被拘押，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被强送洗脑班受迫害，以致其夫离女散，被迫流离失所，长期有家不能回；狱中曾遭到野蛮灌食、串“糖葫芦”、戴支棍儿脚镣、灌盐水、上大挂、奴工等虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其及法轮功好友任小梅一同准备搭乘往返扎兰屯市往返莫旗的大客车时，突遭莫旗客运站乘警拦截，在拒绝其手机被扫码、身份证被检查之后，很快二人被赶来的当地警方非法抓走，后被刑拘于内蒙古阿荣旗看守所；之后，被扎兰屯市检察院以涉嫌邪教罪转正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其二人案在扎兰屯市法院被以网络视频方式开庭受审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其被该法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日；</b>同案任小梅亦被该法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日已刑满释放。赵淑芝目前在内蒙古自治区第一女子监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵维凯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">太原郇城归正基督教会同工。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生。他跟教会传道人安彦魁是好搭档。他俩从小就是好友，后来又一起到王怡牧师创办的成都华西神学院读神学，又一起回到太原服侍教会。赵维凯和妻子李鑫有三个孩子，为了不让孩子接受无神论洗脑教育，他们坚持在家教育孩子，因此多次被民宗局、教委、国宝等有关部门上门约谈，以抓捕相威胁强迫他送孩子上公立学校，被赵维凯拒绝。今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日赵维凯被警察以“宗教诱骗”之名传唤和抄家，他的妻子李鑫也在同一天被传唤。后妻子李鑫获释，但赵维凯却被处以行政拘留约十五天的处罚。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日又被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被正式批捕。据家属收到的逮捕通知书，大致内容是：经文水县检察院批准，由文水县公安局逮捕，羁押在方山县看守所。罪名是所谓“非法持有宣扬恐怖主义极端主义物品”。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵西娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市武功县法轮功学员。王平创<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，妻子赵西娟<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日生，都是陕西咸阳市武功县普集镇义老村人，近年在西安做生意维持生活。王平创曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被劳教迫害，在枣子河劳教所受尽酷刑，被关笼子、夏天暴晒、冬天被浇凉水、做奴工、被牢头暴打等，他一度被迫害致生命垂危。由于警察多次上门骚扰，王平创夫妻被迫流离失所在外。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，王平创夫妻骑电动车在本市公交站牌上粘贴 “法轮大法好”，遭人举报。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日夫妻俩遭周至县公安局和长安区郭杜镇派出所抓捕，参与的警察有<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多人，并抄家。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span>王平创、赵西娟夫妇在西安遭抓捕关押构陷近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">, </span>于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被雁塔区法院法官分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，共勒索<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万惩金。两人不服判决，已上诉至西安市中级法院。目前王平创被关押在西安市安康医院，赵西娟被关押在西安市看守所，两处均以疫情为由不让会见。赵西娟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-%E7%8E%8B%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%9B%E3%80%81%E8%B5%B5%E8%A5%BF%E5%A8%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-441327.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-%E7%8E%8B%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%9B%E3%80%81%E8%B5%B5%E8%A5%BF%E5%A8%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-441327.html</span></b></a></span><b 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">赵秀娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，刘社红和妻子赵秀娟在荆州市被抓捕，被关押在荆州市荆州区西门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉，刘社红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，妻子赵秀娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林长春市农安县法轮功学员。一名退休的高中教师，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>周岁。她于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被当地国保公安局抓捕、抄家，被关押、构陷至今已经<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，遭庭审，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，接到判决书，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。其不服已上诉，长春市中级法院已立案。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/15/%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E5%86%9C%E5%AE%89%E8%B5%B5%E7%A7%80%E5%85%B0%E4%B8%8A%E8%AF%89-430827.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日晚赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被警察等非法闯入各自的家中抓捕的。赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷被关押在安达看守所。后获悉裴玉凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，陈景捷被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。赵秀芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵颜华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，系北京首安消防公司工程师。赵颜华于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，被李桥派出所警察抓捕，当晚送往顺义看守所。关押十个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被北京市顺义区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金三千元。判决书声称：“本院依法组成合议庭，公开开庭审理了本案。”却不让家人亲属参与旁听。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵昭荃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省泸州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年生，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已年<span lang="EN-US">83</span>岁。赵昭荃是泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇乡镇小学退休教师。她因修炼法轮功坚定信仰，不懈地向民众讲清真相，仅<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共迫害法轮功开始至<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年间，她就遭到<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次拘留所拘留，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被关看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被关洗脑班迫害，被劳教两年。她还遭到高额罚款，剥夺退休金，不予转正等严重的经济迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年她被秘密庭审两次、判刑两年<span lang="EN-US">06</span>个月（监外执行），而今又被判刑两年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被泸州市江阳区法院人员以“体检”为由将她从家中带走后一直没有回家。后来从她写回来的家书中得知，当日她被关进了合江看守所隔离。后获悉，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，在泸州市看守所继续关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/23/%E5%B1%85%E5%BF%83%E5%8F%B5%E6%B5%8B%E7%9A%84%E2%80%9C%E4%BD%93%E6%A3%80%E2%80%9D-%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%85%AB%E6%97%AC%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-446610.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/23/%E5%B1%85%E5%BF%83%E5%8F%B5%E6%B5%8B%E7%9A%84%E2%80%9C%E4%BD%93%E6%A3%80%E2%80%9D-%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%85%AB%E6%97%AC%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-446610.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵忠江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江牡丹江市法轮功学员，生于一九五三年四月十一日，牡丹江市爱民区北安镇人，一九九七年三月开始修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月二十日中共迫害法轮功后，多次遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被抓捕、构陷，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已经从看守所转到监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵作媛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，山东省长岛县黑山乡大濠村 村民。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年赵作媛、骆卫东夫妻二人在本村经营球石厂，赵作媛的母亲葛宏婵为此投资数万元。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，因和生意合伙人<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元的债务纠纷，长岛县法院查封了赵作媛价值百万余元的球石和石料，任由债权人倒卖。赵作媛一家被迫起诉至法院要求债权人赔偿损失，岂料，法院判决赵作媛一家赔偿债权人转运这些球石过程中产生的费用。为了寻求公道，赵作媛、骆卫东和母亲一家三口被迫上访维权。上访期间，夫妇二人关系破裂导致离婚。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日赵作媛被北京市丰台区公安局以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日取保释放。<span lang="EN-US"> 2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日赵作媛被绑架到鸿锦大酒店非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">1</span>天。<span lang="EN-US"> 2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日赵作媛被暴力绑架回黑山岛非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">17</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日赵作媛被网上通缉抓捕，以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日逮捕，现羁押在烟台市看守所。据北京市第二中级人民法院赔偿委员会国家赔偿决定书中显示：<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月间，有人在北京南站以打标牌、拍照，并将照片上传到境外互联网网站的手段制造影响。该案经丰台分局侦查发现，赵作媛有重大嫌疑。经丰台分局口头传唤、讯问后，以寻衅滋事罪将其刑事拘留。对赵作媛的拘留符合法律规定的条件和程序，对赵作媛所提赔偿请求不予支持。丰台看守所不许家人为其存钱、存物，导致其受凉后落下腰疼、腹痛等疾病。在暴力劫访过程中被勒脖子，造成脖子发生病变肿大，至今未愈。在非法拘禁期间手机信号被屏蔽。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，赵作媛被烟台市蓬莱区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/46.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肇淑芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古呼伦贝尔市莫力达瓦达斡尔族自治旗（莫旗）法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。满族，以前在呼伦贝尔市莫旗中心商店工作。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始修炼法轮大法。肇淑芝坚持法轮功，遭中共邪党<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次关押、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次判刑、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次洗脑班迫害，死里逃生，夫离女散，被迫流离失所，有家不能回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，肇淑芝和扎兰屯市法轮功学员任小梅，乘坐由扎兰屯市往返莫旗的大客车，在莫旗客运站被乘警拦截，要求手机扫码、检查身份证，遭到拒绝，之后，他们给公安局打电话，公安警察来了之后，开始给肇淑芝和任小梅照相，直接把她们抓捕到内蒙古阿荣旗看守所非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，肇淑芝被非法开庭（视频开庭），并被非法勒索两万元人民币。任晓梅被非法勒索两千元。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，任小梅被非法判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，从阿荣旗看守所出来时强迫签字。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，肇淑芝被扎兰屯市法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，抓捕到内蒙古呼和浩特第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>女子监狱。目前在呼和浩特第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>女子监狱遭受迫害。这是肇淑芝第<span lang="EN-US">9</span>次遭受中共抓捕迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郑大海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连中山区法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在家中被抓捕，遭抄家，羁押于大连姚家看守所，后被视频开庭。近日获悉，郑大海被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b
