lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-440219.html#2231821424-2</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">钟兴秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，传授打印、刻录、装订技术等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在与他人搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被江西省武宁县人民法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟义芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，攀枝花市攀钢集团公司第二机械厂退休工人，法轮功学员。自从中共开始迫害法轮功后，钟义芳非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年钟义芳被判刑八年，于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被关押到四川省龙泉驿女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才出狱回家<span lang="EN-US">.2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月又遭中共当局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，钟义芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。她现在被迫害得出现严重的尿毒症，骨瘦如柴，肚子肿的老大，每天看守所给她打针。生命健康令人担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周彩凡<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省萍乡市安源区高坑镇维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，江西省萍乡市安源区高坑镇居民周彩凡，因去萍乡市信访局上访后，回到家里就被政府的社区工作人员绑架到萍矿总医院高坑院区精神科，进行所谓“精神病强制治疗”。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，一些周彩凡的朋友去医院，要求看望周彩凡，但精神病医生不允许探望。他们问医生把周彩凡当做精神病患者强制收院治疗，有没有家属签字同意。该医生说强制治疗是不需要监护人同意的。周彩凡的朋友们说周彩凡没有精神病，是正常人。而该医生说周彩凡有精神病，因为她为她死去的妹妹上访，她老说她妹妹是被害死的，她老是去上访，老是骂人，妨碍公共秩序。该医生表示，这是政府社区工作人员送来的，他们要求医院对周彩凡强制治疗。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周德元</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：长沙市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁，家住在长沙市左家塘附近的烟草公司宿舍。从一九九八年，周德元开始修炼法轮功。她是一位开朗的常德人，用湖南人都能听懂的常德话和人们交流。从常德市轴承厂退休后，她与家人迁居到了长沙。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，周德元被抓捕，十五天行政拘留结束，又被关押在长沙市第四看守所。后，周德元被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被转送至湖南省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周殿文</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：黑龙江省哈尔滨市依兰县法轮功学员。男，七十多岁，原中煤黑龙江省依兰县达连河煤矿退休工人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份发法轮功台历时，被人诬告，被依兰县公安局国保大队队长杨维兴带人抓捕到看守所。周殿文老人，被关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年末被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，目前在黑龙江省泰来监狱遭受关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。周海燕刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周金霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连维权人士、基督徒。近年来，大连基督徒周金霞坚持不断数十次次到北京中南海前给习近平、彭丽媛传福音，为此多次被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日她在中南海门前举起写着：“神爱世人，呼召习近平、彭丽媛。‘自由、平等、公正、诚信是来自神的，‘无神论’生产罪恶、祸国殃民。公义使邦国高举，罪恶是人民的羞辱！天国近了，你们应当悔改！”随后周金霞被警察扣押、没收了福音信。被大连市公安局于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10 </span>天。而<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，周金霞也曾因在中南海门前传福音被行政拘留过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月周金霞因在冬奥会结束后去新华门拉横幅给习近平传福音，被户籍地警察带回后，已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，关押在大连市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_73.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_73.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">周克铭：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>出生。黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员。鸡西市法轮功学员周克铭在发放法轮功资料时，被人诬告。鸡西市公安局鸡冠区公安分局国保、永昌派出所、铁西派出所采取跟踪、监控手段，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。周克铭刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">周琳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贵州法轮功学员，贵州省威宁县法院退休女法官，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，家住贵阳市观山湖区“美的林城”小区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日因讲法轮功真相遭警察抓捕，后将她关押在贵阳市三江看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底被贵阳市南明区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。周琳随即上诉，贵阳中级法院维持原判。目前她不知被关在何处，亲朋好友都非常担心。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445766.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445766.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周启良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周启良、王传煌、汪黎明三人均系江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，学习、传授打印、刻录、装订等技术，使用具有自动拨号及语音功能的手机给他人打电话等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在共同搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家分别被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被江西省武宁县人民法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其三人均表不服，提起上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前都被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。分别刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。一人独居在贵阳云岩区省政府大院，她父亲是贵州省政府一名老干部。周琴毕业于贵州大学外语学院，后在贵州省教育学院任教，是一名大学英语教师；由于大学期间的一次事故，摔断脚踝造成残疾。周琴<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年以前就修炼法轮功。周琴<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月遭当局抓捕，家人不知。后表姐和友人们多方查询，在离贵阳市很远的“贵阳市三江女子看守所”查到周琴被关押里面。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日周琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，周琴的家人近期收到法院判决书。据说周琴被关押在贵阳羊艾第一女子监狱。因为疫情，家人还没有见到周琴。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周绍山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周世峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，河南省安阳县人，北京锋锐律师事务所主任，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年度、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度“社会公益法律服务先进个人”、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年中国法律援助“优秀援助律师”、<span lang="EN-US"> 2009-2011</span>年度“北京优秀律师”，知名人权律师。自<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年执业以来，曾代理过多起著名的受害人案件，并于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月创立北京锋锐律师事务所，广纳包括王宇、刘晓原、王全章等在内的著名人权律师。<span lang="EN-US"> 2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被北京市警方以“严重扰乱社会秩序”、“教唆、组织、策划、资助他人炒作所谓敏感案件” 等为罪由抓走刑拘，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄。被指定居所监视居住，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被天津市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被天津市第二中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。现羁押在天津市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周维林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽合肥人权捍卫者、工伤致残人士。周维林<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，原安徽省拖拉机厂退休职工，维权网信息员，安徽省维权人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曹顺利人权捍卫者奖获得者。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因工受伤，成为丧失劳动能力的伤残人员，但原所在单位一直不给于办理伤残认定和退休等手续，自此走上维权之路。自<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年期间，因长期坚持实名报导安徽及全国各地多种公权力违法侵权事件，并成为“维权网”信息员，而招致当局的强烈不满和忌恨，曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被合肥警方处以行政拘留，并且多次被警方抄家、传唤、威胁甚至殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，各地维权人士发起声援“安妮失学事件”的活动，周维林因前往进行实时报导，而被合肥警方于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日强行带走，处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又因参与合肥网友聚餐纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>活动，遭到警方的报复性拘留，之后获释；但时至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，合肥警方再次因<span lang="EN-US">64</span>纪念活动而以“涉嫌虚构事实扰乱公共秩序”事由对其进行传唤，并处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，合肥警方第三次以参与声援安妮失学事件，维护安妮受教育权活动为由，将其与张林、李化平、姚诚等维权人士一同拘捕，并以涉嫌“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”而刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被当地检察院以同罪名正式批捕，之后被安徽省合肥市地方法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刑满获释。出狱后仍然在一直坚持为劳工和残疾人维权。周维林于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被合肥市公安局瑶海分局城东派出所（电话：<span lang="EN-US">0551-64483496</span>）秘密抓走了。后获悉遭刑事拘留、逮捕。周维林案已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在合肥开庭审理，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日年获悉：周维林案已宣判，周维林获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周喜云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑州市法轮功学员。女，四十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，周喜云在荆建秋家中做客，她俩一起被荥阳广武派出所警察、荥阳国保大队警察抓捕，被关押在郑州第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在中原区法院南办公区被开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，荆建秋和周喜云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">周秀华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，湖北省武汉法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，周秀华修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，武汉市公安局东西湖区分局又以莫须有的所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”，把周秀华起诉到东西湖区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日她被逮捕。之后关押于武汉市第一拘留所，不久又转到武汉市第一看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被武汉市汉阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">7000</span>元。随后，周秀华不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，武汉市中级法院在不开庭的情况下，做了维持原判的所谓判决。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E6%AD%A6%E6%B1%89%E5%91%A8%E7%A7%80%E5%8D%8E%E4%B8%8A%E8%AF%89-%E4%B8%AD%E7%BA%A7%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-441340.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">周秀丽</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：山西省忻州市代县法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生。周秀丽在去内蒙古探望失去生活自理能力的老母亲期间，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在包头市城区发放法轮功资料时被包头市达茂联合旗公安局国保大队抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被代县公安局执行逮捕并关押在忻州市看守所遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元，给家庭造成很大的压力和伤害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445961.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445961.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周妍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。周研被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周艳波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，周艳波毕业于大连医科大学附属卫校，由国家统一分配到大连开发区医院工作，从事临床护理工作。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年，周艳波开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，没有经过任何法律程序，周艳波被劫持到了马三家劳教所，被劳教两年。遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被国保警察抓捕后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被视频非法开庭，周艳波被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前，周艳波仍被非法关押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省农安县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，家住长春市农安县，常在长春市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，周永杰被长春市朝阳区宽平派出所抓捕。关押在长春市第四看守所。此后家属未得到任何信息。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，周永杰被关押在长春市女子监狱后，家属才得知，她被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州凌海市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，孙继萍与丈夫周永林被中共绑架、关押，劳教，在派出所、看守所、劳教所遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙继萍与丈夫周永林在盘锦市锦采新区大集上告诉人们“法轮大法好”时，被凌海市公安局闫家镇派出所警察绑架，被隔离二十一天后（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），孙继萍被非法关押到锦州市女子看守所，周永林被非法关押到凌海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，凌海市法院对孙继萍与丈夫周永林每人各判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金各一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周玉香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东平度市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>岁生，是平度大泽山镇尹家村一位普通的农村妇女。周玉香<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与外甥女周君、好友展中香一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕并被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，周玉香被青岛市黄岛区法院在即墨市普东看守所，通过视频非法庭审，律师做了有理有据的无罪辩护，最后，周玉香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk52057464"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周育琴</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，周育琴与石雪梅、刘庆强三人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日</b>）；石雪梅被冤判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）。三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周再强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南长沙网民。职业货车司机。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月网上发言支持香港反送中的光复香港、时代革命运动被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，周再强的亲友才在微信发出消息称：长沙公民周再强近期因在推特上发言支持香港反送中运动而被当局突然抓捕，并以寻衅滋事的罪名刑事拘留，目前已经确认被关押于长沙市第一看守所。据了解，周再强有两个匿名推特号，已持续发推三万多条。香港反送中运动爆发后，他一直都非常关注，也自发和转发了很多推文表示关注和支持。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">朱恩华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省昆明市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日生，女。朱恩华女士与母亲杨树珍<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在曲靖家中被国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，母亲杨树珍被枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445958.html%E3%80%81"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445958.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱凤兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，河南省新乡市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午，在新乡市南高村一出租屋内被河南省新乡市公安局国保警察抓捕。被抢走电脑、打印机等大量个人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱凤兰被辉县市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚款一万元。朱凤兰向新乡市中级法院提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，新乡市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，朱凤兰被关押到新乡市第五女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱桂贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东泰安市法轮功信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁的老太太，原泰安市木器厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，朱桂贞和平秀英为了让民众了解法轮大法，在邱家店镇某村，发送法轮功资料，并向路人讲述法轮功受迫害的真相，遭邱家店派出所警察绑架，被关到泰安市看守所。后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，朱桂贞因修炼法轮功，向百姓传播法轮大法，被泰安市泰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏银川市永宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生。大学本科毕业，原宁夏银川市永宁县环境监测中心工作人员，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年底开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，朱海燕多次被抓捕、被关押、劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱海燕等<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名法轮功学员被银川市永宁县公安局恶警抓捕、抄家，朱海燕被关押在银川市看守所，后被银川市永宁县公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院；遭银川市永宁县公安局和银川市西夏区检察院相互勾结迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱惠来：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省湛江市人，广东省湛江市东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，抗强拆维权者，民间誉名“东海岛英雄”，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱惠来父子一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等；其子朱培忍开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随前往和其一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤（其中致当地治安大队副队长死亡）；随后，其立即被警方刑拘和逮捕，但却被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死刑；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判死缓；其不服，继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东省湛江市中级法院再次重审朱惠来父子抗强拆杀官员案，仍判死刑。　<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，广东高院（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>）粤刑终<span lang="EN-US">298</span>号判决书作出终审判决：朱惠来犯故意杀人罪、故意伤害罪，决定执行死刑，缓期二年执行，剥夺政治权利终身，并限制减刑。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱家彩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。朱家彩刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">朱建华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">北京朝阳区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，家住工体附近，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被抓捕，一直被关在昌平东城看守所。后获悉，他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日左右被转到深圳的监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437388.html#22127221922-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">朱明兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省蛟河市白石山镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，法轮功学员朱明兰、刘甲兰、山福莲被镇派出所骗去测核酸，录指纹，随后就被关押到吉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年二月十九日，吉林省蛟河市白石山镇法轮功学员朱明兰、刘甲兰、山福莲被最终判决，分别为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。目前，她们被关押在长春市女子监狱。朱明兰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/11/444764.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/11/444764.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱明容：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，四川乐山市人，法轮功学员。因坚持修炼法轮大法、屡遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，朱明容女士到北京上访，在广元被劫持回乐山，被拘留<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天；同年至<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。共计坐牢<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日因宣讲法轮功，被乐山市公安抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/14/443532.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/14/443532.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱培忍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省湛江市人，广东湛江东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，“东海岛英雄”，抗暴维权者。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱培忍和其父一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其父田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等，其父被严重殴打；其开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随上前与父亲一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤，其随被警方拘捕，但被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死缓。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判为无期徒刑。其依然不服，继续上诉，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日湛江市中级法院再审朱惠来父子抗暴杀官案，仍为无期徒刑。目前被关押地点不详。其在看守所惨遭酷刑，肝部被打裂，生殖器被打烂，牙齿被打掉，为此曾被送医院抢救。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱素荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，家住河北保定蠡县鲍墟乡东孟尝村，在中孟尝小学任教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，正在学校上课的朱素荣，突然被鲍墟乡派出所警察骚扰，他们并尾随至家中抄家捕人，当天朱素荣就被送至保定看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被高阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、勒索罚金五万元，朱素荣已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">朱孝清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省嫩江市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，家住黑龙江省嫩江市<span lang="EN-US">7</span>星泡农场。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年修炼法轮功。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共集团迫害法轮功后，朱孝清坚持信仰，遭到中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，朱孝清因发放法轮功法轮功资料，被警方抓捕。后被监视居住半年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，朱孝清被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/12/%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9C%B1%E5%AD%9D%E6%B8%85%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441202.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/12/%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9C%B1%E5%AD%9D%E6%B8%85%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441202.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱玉芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，江西省萍乡市人，曾为私营企业主，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因所经营的店铺被时任萍乡市副市长唐湘萍及其丈夫房管局局长家族开办的房地产公司强拆，而走上维权之路。萍乡地方政府在腐败势力操纵下，将朱玉芳作为重点维稳控制和打击对象。在维权过程中，朱玉芳多次被绑架、关黑监狱、遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因在北京上访维权而被非法拘禁于北京市大兴区某黑监狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，并被与两个男看守放在一个房间，险遭人身侵犯；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因再次在北京上访而被警方抓捕，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，后又被送至北京市久敬庄非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天，而后被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾被地方当局长期非法软禁家中，房门被反锁，不准出门；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，因到北京上访而被北京市公安局朝阳警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后因其怀孕又于同日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因其身穿访民反腐文化衫到联合国驻京开发署呼吁要求人权，而被北京市朝阳区警方再次刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因持续在北京上访维权，并将自己遭受迫害经历发于网上，再度被北京警方以“查获访民身份”为由抓走和交由萍乡驻京办事处将其遣返原籍，于遣返当日被萍乡市安源区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，并关押于萍乡市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被江西省萍乡市安源区法院一审以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，经江西省萍乡市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，后送江西省女子监狱服刑；出狱后，其一直就被枉法冤判申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因又到到江西省高级法院申诉，遭拒，随就在法院门外举牌呼吁；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（即世界人权日），其突遭失联，后知被江西省萍乡市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，不到一周即被萍乡市安源区检察院批准逮捕，羁押在萍乡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_22.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_22.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱宇飙：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，广东省人，原广州地铁小额贷款有限公司职员，原广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所、广东恒益律师事务所执业律师，广东省第一个公开为法轮功信仰者作无罪辩护的正义律师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。学生时代，曾就读于广东省中山大学法学专业；法学硕士毕业后，先后曾就职于广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所和广东恒益律师事务所，作执业律师；因为经常热心为弱势群体当事人作代理辩护律师，并以低价或折价收费，甚至不计报酬，所以深受社会大众及业界同仁称许、好评；但因其练习和信仰法轮功而屡遭政府打压逼迫，遂被迫多次转换律所，直至最终其律师执业证被广东司法当局吊销；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾分别为三名法轮功信仰者做无罪辩护，因其法庭辩护词精彩绝伦，堪称经典，顿令中共法庭大为震惊和难堪，随后即被广东司法当局称为“反革命”，将其列为广东省公安厅要维稳严控的“头号人物”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其突然被广州市警方野蛮抓捕，后被枉法处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，送广州市第三劳教所关押；关押期间，曾遭多次酷刑折磨，如“坐老虎凳”、“架飞机”、用湿毛巾盖脸窒息、水淹、在冷天灌凉水、鞭打手指及脚趾、不准睡觉，等等；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，劳教释放后，因其律师证被广州当局故意拖延办理，对其工作和日常生活造成极大不便；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其第二次被广州市海珠区新港派出所警方莫名抓捕、刑拘，家遭查抄，后被广州市海珠区法院以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并送广东省北江监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，虽是其刑满获释日，但又被转送到广东省三水洗脑班非法关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，再次被广州市海珠区警方十余人闯入抄家，搜走几本其个人阅读的法轮功书籍之后，随即将其绑架到一不知名的法轮功洗脑班关押；据悉，自其被抓至今，家人一直无法知其更多信息。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱兆水：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省舒兰市吉舒镇法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。曾被非法劳教一年多。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚被当地警方抓捕、关押；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬获悉，朱兆水被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">朱忠富：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南楚雄州法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US"> 1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁，四川攀枝花市规划建筑设计研究院退休职工。在中共对法轮功持续至今<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年的迫害中，他曾于<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日朱忠富与妻子李卫萍因向人发法轮功资料，被楚雄国保警察抓捕、抄家。被关押在楚雄市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445959.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445959.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱作亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，浙江省金华市金东区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，朱作亮曾被中共抓捕，关押，并分别在南宁市看守所、杭州市看守所、十里坪劳教所及监狱遭多种酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾被“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”头目曹秋水等抓捕到金华双龙洗脑班迫害，之后又被劫持到金华市看守所，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱作亮被劫入浙江省第四监狱继续迫害<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月以后，在中共邪党的“清零”迫害中，被要求签“三书”（即诬陷法轮功，并签放弃法轮功的保证），被其当面拒绝，随因坚持信仰被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被庭审。据悉，朱作亮被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在金华看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AD%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%B5%99%E6%B1%9F%E6%9C%B1%E4%BD%9C%E4%BA%AE%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430300.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AD%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%B5%99%E6%B1%9F%E6%9C%B1%E4%BD%9C%E4%BA%AE%E</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">祝亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉市黄陂区法轮功学员，祝亚是个残疾人，家住武汉市黄陂区前川街，丈夫早逝，她与女儿相依为命。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，祝亚去买菜，被便衣警察拦截。这次抓捕祝亚是由省城“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”亲自操控、指使的，他们闯进家中抄家。武汉市黄陂区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日庭审，被秘密枉判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠扎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县求吉玛乡索日玛村人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾被当局以不详政治罪名抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被警方以涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁寿辰活动”为罪由，从其僧舍强行带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其已被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 119.25pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠玛别克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>穆汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，新疆阿尔泰市人，阿尔泰市喀拉希力克乡武装部官员，哈萨克族政治犯。曾因被新疆中共当局指控在聊天工具微信“乱说话”，“泄漏中共党内机密”，而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被阿尔泰市警方刑拘、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，获悉近期已被新疆阿尔泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。据称，其原本在上海读大学的儿子因父亲被判刑，竟遭株连，被校方勒令退学，现已回到新疆家中。其妻子古丽加丽拉也因受牵连，原本在乡政府卫生院工作，也因此被辞退，他本人在银行的<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元人民币积蓄遭罚没，家里的<span lang="EN-US">50</span>头牛也被政府没收。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庄惠清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，广东省揭阳市普宁市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月生，家住普宁市南径镇南径村。庄惠清、陈泳慧<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日上午在普宁市梅塘镇讲法轮功，被梅塘派出所抓捕。随后，梅塘派出所等有关部门到她们家抄家，抢走私人物品。庄惠清、陈泳惠<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日已被送往普宁市看守所关押、构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月庄惠清被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，陈泳慧被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，她们已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被关押到广东女子监狱。庄惠清刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/5/442103.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/5/442103.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">庄友布：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，福建省宁德市福鼎县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，庄友布被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，庄友布被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">卓顺珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省孝感市安陆市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，卓顺珍在安陆市木梓江河村讲法轮功真相，遭木梓村村书记骚扰、拍照、恶告。随后遭到不断司法迫害，被迫离家远走他乡。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年在四川被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日遭安陆市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/26/445443.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/26/445443.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹华兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，今年<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，重庆长寿区法轮功学员，原重庆长寿农机公司退休职工，邹华兰因修炼法轮功曾多次遭受迫害：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次判刑，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被关洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次关押在看守所将近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，中共政法委书记郭声琨到重庆开会，要求对跨区域活动的维权人士、法轮功学员等要重点打击。重庆市长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保为了完成所谓的“政治任务”，也为了捞取升官资本，开始寻找他们的下手目标。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，邹华兰在贵州结束冤狱回家。因为这段被外省判刑的经历，邹华兰成了长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保的迫害对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，长寿区国保支队指使晏家街道派出所警察，到贵州去调查邹华兰被构陷的案子，作为再次迫害的“证据”。然后，又以监控摄像头摄到邹华兰在晏家街道发台历为借口，晏家派出所几个警察，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">33</span>日，闯入邹华兰家中，把邹华兰抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，邹华兰被逮捕，后被关押在长寿区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，邹华兰被重庆市江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹佩霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东东营法轮功学员。耿录堂、邹佩霞老夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已年过七旬，家住东营市胜利油田孤岛采油厂芙蓉小区。修炼大法前，夫妻俩身体很不好，耿录堂还患有高血压等疾病。一九九六年前后，老俩口修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，老俩口去河口地区赶集，向人宣传法轮功，遭人恶告，东营市河口区国保大队下属的义和镇派出所警察，于当天抓捕了夫妇俩。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后耿录堂、邹佩霞夫妇均被东营市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被勒索罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邹幸彤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">Tonyee Chow Hang-tung</span>，原英属香港籍人，现中华人民共和国（香港）公民，香港大律师，原香港支联会副主席，第<span lang="EN-US">35</span>届“中国杰出民主人士奖”荣获者，民主人权斗士，社会活动家，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于英国剑桥大学哈默顿学院物理学系，毕业后又在香港大学专业进修学院研读法律专业，而后成为一名香港执业大律师；自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因致力于中国的民主人权事业， 随开始担任香港支联会（即香港市民支持爱国民主运动联合会）副主席，期间，曾积极推动和举办了每年的维多利亚公园（简称“维园”）<span lang="EN-US">64</span>纪念烛光晚会；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，当李卓人、何俊仁等香港民主前辈和支联会高层相继 遭遇中共香港政府的迫害身陷囹圄时，其勇敢的站出来，成为继续组织香港市民纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>活动的主要领导者；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，在中共主导下的港版“国安法”管控下，支联会被香港警方以防疫（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>冠状病毒疾病，<span lang="EN-US">COVID-19</span>）为由禁止在维园举行当晚的悼念<span lang="EN-US">64 </span>烛光晚会；针此，支联会立即提起上诉，但因上诉很快被驳回，故其公开表态自己会以个人名义到场纪念；次日，即被警方以涉嫌“宣传未经批准集结”为由拘捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，暂获取保候审，但<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又因拒绝在限期内向香港国安处提交支联会的文件而再被港警拘捕；次日，又被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”和支联会主席李卓人、副主席何俊仁等共计<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人一起正式起诉，被指控因在社交网络和媒体发表意在鼓动民众参与未经批准的六四集会言论，其等言行已触犯港版《国安法》的相关法令，故应予量刑；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其一行<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人案被香港法院统一宣判，其中，其被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”和<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“煽动他人参与纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>集会罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年（<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月）；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又被香港法院以<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年两次 “煽动他人参与纪念六四集会罪” 判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">15</span>个月）；因先后两次判决的一部分刑期同时执行，故其最后实际执行刑期<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">22</span>个月 ）；据悉，庭审中其拒绝认罪，坚称其发帖与撰文旨在呼吁人们勿忘六四，并非鼓动众人聚集闹事。目前在香港监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_69.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_69.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">左洪涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山海关区检察院侦监科科长陈铁忠对左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。左洪涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">结束语：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告是一份月度动态报告，这是第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">82</span></b>期，肯定仍然会有遗漏和信息滞后的情况。希望大陆各地的人权捍卫者积极补充，请将符合本报告标准而未统计人员情况、以及本报告名单人员的最新情况提供给我们，以便使以后的报告更加翔实和完善。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">维权网联系方法：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">附录：</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人的名单及</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">简历</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨靖波、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font:
