mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张文涛、赵军、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姜野飞</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、边彦娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北辛集法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，河北省辛集市南智邱镇南棚村李月棉和辛集市马庄乡北营村郑艳梅、边彦娟因讲法轮功真相被大屯派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日第二次开庭，律师又充分的做了无罪辩护，法官说结果要等通知，然后因为疫情一直到三月份律师才得知结果，三人都被判刑，刑期分别为：李月棉<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元；郑艳梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">9</span>千元；边彦娟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。后得知，这三名法轮功学员已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日都被关押到石家庄女子监狱服刑。边彦娟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、蔡俊平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南许昌市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，家住许昌市建安区苏桥镇蔡庄村，为人淳朴善良，踏实能干，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年初，他开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，许昌市建安区国保大队与苏桥镇派出所等多个警察，到苏桥镇蔡庄村蔡俊平的家，非法抄家，抄走计算机、打印机等私人物品，将蔡俊平抓捕关押到许昌市建安区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，蔡俊平被许昌市魏都区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在河南新密监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、陈呈香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北监利访民李树南妻子。李树南：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省荆州市监利县白螺镇人，监利县白螺镇五里庙村村民，司法不公举报人，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李树南、陈呈香夫妇被荆州市监利县警方从家中突然带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，知其早已被转正式批捕，其案现已被检察院以同罪由移交至湖北省荆州市监利县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时，李树南、陈呈香夫妻二人寻衅滋事案，在监利县检察院视频开庭，被告人大女儿李艳华，律师尚满庆、杨高华到达现场。在庭审过程中，检察官以其夫妻二人多次扰乱公共秩序、敲诈勒索予以定罪，建议给予<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年刑期。未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，李树南、陈呈香夫妇分别获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。目前二人均被羁押于荆州市监利县看守所。陈呈香刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陈昱昊：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1993</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，广东省汕头市人，网名“宫本美代子”，“萌娘百科”巡查员，音<span lang="EN-US">MAD</span>作者与<span lang="EN-US">BB</span>剧场（即以<span lang="EN-US">BB/GB</span>素材等制作的动画）作者，恶俗维基管理员，哲学中文维基行政员，人称“陈导师”，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于南方医科大学，并在南方医院进行实习；大学毕业后，因转行在“萌娘百科”上当巡查员，曾上传过大量含恶俗维基内容的相关文件，并积极撰写页面，故为恶俗维基的美化宣传立下了汗马功劳。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在<span lang="EN-US">B</span>站（即<span lang="EN-US">bilibili</span>（<span lang="EN-US">NASDAQ</span>：<span lang="EN-US">BILI</span>），全称为“哔哩哔哩弹幕网”的简称，创立于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，现为中国大陆境内最大的年轻人潮流文化娱乐小区）的音乐区发布过“迫真东方”同人的音乐，即纪念某次学运歌曲的倒放混响版本，故有较高人气度。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾因中文曲奇（即大部分东方合同常用的动画企画视频及由此产生的网络模因的概称）维基和中文银梦（即中文与互联网界相契合的淫梦百科全书及相应文化简称）维基陆续建立，随经商议后暂返恶俗维基作编辑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因“恶俗维基”与多家恶俗圈网热发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的相关讯息（含户籍、照片等个人信息），遂立遭当局严厉打压。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部成立项目组，开始对全国各恶俗网站会员实施统一大抓捕，但后经严格审讯，发觉其成员大多年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，遂准予各地警方纷纷放人，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功嘉奖，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，且上报公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把其所辖维基成员全部抓捕。在当时，其虽并非两个网站的核心人物，亦未参与过“支纳维基”挂网披露习近平等国家领导人亲属讯息的活动，但仍于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被广东省茂名市警方予以抓捕，后被暂短指定居所监视居住和刑拘。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”在广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，涉案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，其被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。其等均表不服，已提起上诉，二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、程西江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">济南市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日当天，济南市铁路派出所再次抓捕法轮功学员尹峰，警察同时对最近曾与尹峰有过交往的、居住在朝阳小区的法轮功学员程西江陈连美等法轮功学员抄家、抓捕。程西江被抄走打印机、电脑、大法书籍和一些《九评》、《共产主义的终极目的》等物品和书籍。当日下午，尹峰被逼交<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金后回家。程西江、陈连美被关押在济南铁路看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被秘密审判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、付秋荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省烟台市龙口法轮功学员。袁玉芹、姚新人、付秋荣<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被国保跟踪抓捕。身强力壮的姚新人<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，在龙口市张家沟看守所「突发」脑溢血，在龙口市人民医院被做开颅手术和气管切开术，龙口公安安插四五个警察在医院进行二十四小时监视。姚新人成植物人状态。龙口公安、国保、看守所至今没给家属任何解释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，袁玉芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，付秋荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。付秋荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">7</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、付文花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖北省南漳县武安镇人，因为<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月她儿子付学刚遭遇车祸后对方不承担医疗费，交警不予处理让他到法院起诉而上访，上访期间被对此殴打、拘留<span lang="EN-US">,</span>曾在拘留所被迫割腕自尽。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花在京被南漳县武安镇派出所强行押回后被拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，关押在南漳拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午武安镇政府李才明书记和几个不明身份人员强行将付文花从南漳拘留所抬出来塞进车里带走，进行私自拘禁、酷刑虐待并讹诈，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花被折磨至昏死而丢在路旁被人救起。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，付文花被南漳县公安局抓走，关押在湖北省南漳县看守所。付文花于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点在南漳县法院秘密开庭，被以寻衅滋事罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、胡新成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省太原市籍人，媒体人，公民记录者和作家，原《湖北法制报》副总编辑，公益行动践行者，“大病免费医疗 你我每日一呼”运动推广人，维权举报人，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。曾因长期从事法制媒体工作，走遍了全国<span lang="EN-US">200</span>多个县市，接触有数百个大小各类案件，写过近千篇曝光文章和举报、投诉材料，故而使得很多贪官落马，奸商归案，并为很多读者挽回了积极损失、维护了合法权益；后又因热心参与社会公益事业，随开始致力于宣传推广“大病免费医疗，你我每日一呼”，并公开表明：“我愿意义务为各位网友代写各种材料，并提供解决问题的最佳途径和方案”；此外，因其还称自己将完成一部名叫《中国访民调查》的书籍，内中专门收录一些通过司法没有解决、导致民众上访的案例，分析访民产生的原因和期间经历的磨难，以期能对以后如何改革司法机制做出参考，故此引发社会极大热议；然而却令当局极为不适，将其定为需要维稳、监控的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因其订购了几百条纯棉毛巾，准备走遍全国，赠予案件所在地和沿途经过城市的朋友们，并欲征集一万个“大病免费医疗”的公民签名书，送交至全国人大，但却突遭失踪；后知其为推广“大病免费医疗，你我每日一呼”行动行走到广西壮族自治区省来宾市武宣县时，被警方抓捕，遭强迫失踪；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被山西省太原市警方以涉嫌“宣扬恐怖主义、极端主义、煽动实施恐怖活动“三项罪正式逮捕。被羁押于山西省太原市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月取保获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_89.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_89.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_7.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_7.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、黄日新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东东莞法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，大学本科毕业。因讲述法轮功被迫害真相，黄日新<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被东莞市第二法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日才从刑满出狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，黄日新在自己创办公司的总经理办公室内，向到其公司应聘面试人员讲述法轮功真相，被恶意举报，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，黄日新被东莞市第二法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">10</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、焦孟娇<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，焦孟娇等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括焦孟娇在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。焦孟娇被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19"><b 0pt;">11</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、李佳轩<span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李伟涛：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王永生<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罗丽<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、汤显贺<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、国世游<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、谷林杰<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并附带罚款，其中五人已上诉。李伟涛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">13</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、梁香姣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，湖北省武汉市蔡甸区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，梁香姣被汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押到武汉女子监狱，遭酷刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，梁香姣被几个便衣警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留。被羁押在武汉市第一看守所。经过一年多的构陷，据悉武汉市汉阳区法院将于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日晚上六点庭审梁香姣。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在被关押一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午两点半，在武汉市汉阳区法院庭审据悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">14</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、廖光慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川绵阳市涪城区新华厂家属区法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日下午，廖光慧，被十几个身穿便衣的彪形大汉（后了解是花园派出所警察）突然闯入家中，未出示任何搜捕证和身份证明等，就强行控制家人自由行动，像土匪一样抄家近三个小时之久，强行抢走私人物品：笔记本计算机</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">台，手机、打印机、刻录机、现金几百元，大法书籍、大法师父法像等个人物品。廖光慧被关押在绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日被绵阳市涪城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金三千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、刘学荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省烟台市牟平区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。刘学荣老人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午在牟平区集贸市场发法轮大法资料，被便衣警察绑架，随后被关押到烟台市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，牟平区公检法机构秘密对老人判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被关押到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、潘学明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连市甘井子区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月大连市政法委、六一零借口“七十年大庆”维稳，操控国保大队等长期对法轮功学员监视、监听、跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日抓捕了至少大连七位法轮功学员。当天早晨，潘学明在家中被凌水派出所警察抓捕、抄家，抢劫走电脑、打印机、大法书籍。因身体状况，监狱不收，潘学明至今仍被羁押在大连姚家看守所。潘学明被关在看守所<span lang="EN-US">4-12</span>监室，吃喝拉撒睡都在监室。身陷囹圄，暗无天日的铁窗生活，加之办案人员的刑讯逼供，导致潘学明身体出现严重病态，经常咳嗽，肺部呼吸困难。在不适合羁押的情况下，仍遭高新园区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">17</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、邱华芝<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span></span><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，居住在广东省东莞市横沥镇。她因为向民众讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被广州市东山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日傍晚，邱华芝、张晓洲母女到广州市增城区新塘镇万达广场购物，在一楼停车场发放了几份法轮功资料，被监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邱华芝、张晓洲母女在邱华芝位于东莞市横沥镇的家中被抓捕，随后母女均被抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，邱华芝被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；张晓洲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。邱华芝刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/20/%E5%B9%BF%E5%B7%9E%E9%82%B1%E5%8D%8E%E8%8A%9D%E3%80%81%E5%BC%A0%E6%99%93%E6%B4%B2%E6%AF%8D%E5%A5%B3%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-443856.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;">18</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、盛淑丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛市平度市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，家住青岛平度市祝沟镇祝沟村。盛淑莉遭中共多次抓捕、关押，被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，盛淑莉被平度市祝沟镇派出所伙同平度「<span lang="EN-US">610</span>」抓捕到平度「洗脑班」迫害了<span lang="EN-US">40</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，盛淑莉劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，盛淑莉和另一法轮功学员曲元芝到平度市旧店镇讲真相，遭不明真相的构陷，被抓捕，第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天被抓捕，关押到即墨普东看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，盛淑莉被平度法院秘密庭审、非法判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，盛淑莉和曲元芝到旧店镇北大流河村讲真相，遭不明真相的人构陷，被祝沟镇派出所警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被抓捕到青岛即墨普东看守所关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，祝沟派出所警察又抓捕了盛淑莉<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁的父亲盛松刚，不久盛松刚被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，盛淑莉和曲元芝在青岛即墨普东看守所被青岛市黄岛区法院非法庭审；之后盛淑莉被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，曲元芝被枉判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，盛淑丽被劫入山东省女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">19</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、宋国礼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃省白银市靖远县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。靖远县东湾镇三合村农民，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月修炼法轮功。因张贴法轮功标语，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，宋国礼在公交车上被靖远县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>绑架。后宋国礼被送到靖远县看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被白银法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金八千元，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被送到甘肃省大沙坪监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">20</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、孙凤仙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：孙凤仙被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">:5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至<span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、吴葛健雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，外称“小吴”，弱势群体维权诉讼代理人，民间公益组织“长沙富能”<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>成员，中国在押政治犯。因积极从事公益维权活动，代理多起维权诉讼案件等，深受大众欢迎；近年来因在参与公益维权同时，与机构其他<span lang="EN-US">CEO</span>成员和海外人道服务机构往来较多，随遭中共当局警觉及严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，因对香港「反送中」抗议有同情言论，<span lang="EN-US"> 7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日随与另两位公益成员一同被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方从公司办公室带走，且被旋即以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；其父已收到他的拘留通知书；据悉，其事先委托代理律师向长沙市国家安全局了解详情遭拒，仅告知被控涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”，原因不明，疑与香港正在进行的反送中风潮有关；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。后遭强迫辞退自己做律师的父亲代理，当局强行派官派律师，目前已经进入司法审判阶段并且已经开庭审理，可家人对案情却一无所知。目前被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能发起人程渊的妻子施明磊综合各渠道信息，获悉长沙公益仨程渊、吴葛健雄、刘大志三人已在北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午被长沙市中级法院判决，吴葛健雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刘大志被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，程渊刑期<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。吴葛健雄<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被转去赤山监狱服刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html"><b lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" minor-fareast;">28</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、许传香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东日照市莒县乔山镇郝家洪沟法轮功学员。许传香<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在招贤镇招贤大街张贴法轮功真相资料时，被招贤镇派出所警察抓捕。警察抄家，抢走<span lang="EN-US">3</span>本大法书籍、计算机主机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台、笔记本计算机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台，扣押踏板摩托车<span lang="EN-US">1</span>辆，并将许传香关押到莒县拘留所拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月份将从日照看守所转往济南山东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">29</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、杨桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，家住青岛市崂山北宅。法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，曾被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，杨桂芳在城阳区集市被城阳区分局夏庄派出所抓捕抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，青岛即墨法院对杨桂芳开庭。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，青岛即墨法院当庭判刑杨桂芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月刑期，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">30</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、杨靖波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功学员杨靖波、武存仙、倪会仙由于在小区粘贴「法轮大法好！真善忍好！」不干胶，和向住户赠送「天赐洪福」法轮功小册子，被安宁市金方街道办事处不法人员告发，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被安宁市国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被西山区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，杨靖波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，岳长友和纪凤霞到楼区为居民免费发大法法轮功资料，岳长友被警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：张敬元被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张敬元被送到公主岭监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><b mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">33</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、张鹏柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邓玉林、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。张鹏柱刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">34</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、张文涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张文涛<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">35</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、赵军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，被国安抓捕控制后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">36</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、姜野飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川成都人，约生于<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年，民主人士，人权捍卫者，参加过“八九”学运，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年“汶川地震”后又积极参与维权活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年“六四”前夕，姜野飞在曼谷中共国大使馆门前参与纪念“六四”二十周年静坐活动，被泰国当局抓捕，关押近三年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日与董广平逃亡泰国，二人同被泰国警方在其持有联合国难民署签发的“庇护申请者证明书”（实为保护信）的前提下又以涉嫌“偷渡罪”抓捕，并关押于泰国曼谷市沙吞移民监狱；后经各方民主人士努力和紧急呼吁，被联合国难民署获悉，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日答应拟启动紧急通道，力促使其全家获准难民身份；但<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日仍被中共当局以“非法越境罪”遣送押解回国。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被重庆公安局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”、“组织他人偷越国境罪”逮捕。目前羁押于重庆市第二看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，重庆市第一中级法院对姜野飞颠覆国家政权、偷越国境案宣判，认定姜野飞犯颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，犯偷越国境罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金一千元（人民币，下同），决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金一千元。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span
